```typescript
// shared/api/uma/types.ts

/** Request for JSQL select endpoint */
export interface SelectRequest {
  jsql: Record<string, unknown>;
  params?: Record<string, unknown> | null;
}

/** Response for select endpoint */
export interface SelectResponse {
  meta: ColumnMeta[];
  data: Record<string, unknown>[];
}

/** Column metadata from UMA */
export interface ColumnMeta {
  name: string;
  type: string;
  nullable: boolean;
  qualified_name: string;
}

/** Request for SQL to JSQL transformation */
export interface SQL2JSQLRequest {
  data: string; // SQL query string
  dialect: string; // SQL dialect (generic, postgresql, mysql, sqlite, etc.)
}

/** Request for JSQL to SQL transformation */
export interface JSQL2SQLRequest {
  data: Record<string, unknown>; // JSQL query dictionary
  dialect: string; // SQL dialect (generic, postgresql, mysql, sqlite, etc.)
}

/** Request for entity list endpoint */
export interface EntityListRequest {
  namespace?: string | null;
}

/** Response for entity list endpoint */
export interface EntityListResponse {
  entities: string[];
}

/** Request for entity details endpoint */
export interface EntityDetailsRequest {
  entity_name: string;
}

/** Entity metadata */
export interface EntityMetadata {
  name: string;
  namespace?: string;
  columns: ColumnInfo[];
  indexes?: string[];
  constraints?: ConstraintInfo[];
}

/** Column information */
export interface ColumnInfo {
  name: string;
  type: string;
  nullable: boolean;
  primary_key: boolean;
  default_value?: unknown;
  qualified_name: string;
}

/** Constraint information */
export interface ConstraintInfo {
  name: string;
  type: 'PRIMARY_KEY' | 'FOREIGN_KEY' | 'UNIQUE' | 'CHECK';
  columns: string[];
  references?: {
    table: string;
    columns: string[];
  };
}

/** Error response */
export interface ErrorResponse {
  id: string; // Exception type (e.g., "UMAAccessDeniedError")
  message: string; // User-friendly error message
  details: Record<string, unknown>; // Structured details for frontend processing
}

// entities/query/model/types.ts

/** Query types */
export interface Query {
  id: string;
  type: 'sql' | 'jsql';
  sql?: string;
  jsql?: Record<string, unknown>;
  dialect: string;
  created_at: string;
  updated_at: string;
}

export interface SqlQuery extends Query {
  type: 'sql';
  sql: string;
}

export interface JsqlQuery extends Query {
  type: 'jsql';
  jsql: Record<string, unknown>;
}

// entities/history/model/types.ts

/** History item */
export interface HistoryItem {
  id: string;
  type: 'sql' | 'jsql';
  query: string | Record<string, unknown>;
  executed_at: string;
  execution_time?: number; // milliseconds
  rows_affected?: number;
  is_favorite: boolean;
}

/** History filters */
export interface HistoryFilters {
  type?: 'sql' | 'jsql' | 'all';
  date_from?: string;
  date_to?: string;
  favorites_only?: boolean;
}
```

```typescript
// shared/lib/fetch/fetch-client.ts
import { type FetchOptions, type FetchResponse } from './types';

const DEFAULT_TIMEOUT = 30000; // 30 —Å–µ–∫—É–Ω–¥

export class FetchClient {
  private baseURL: string;
  private defaultHeaders: Record<string, string>;
  private timeout: number;

  constructor(
    baseURL: string,
    options?: { timeout?: number; headers?: Record<string, string> }
  ) {
    this.baseURL = baseURL.replace(/\/$/, '');
    this.defaultHeaders = options?.headers || {
      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
    };
    this.timeout = options?.timeout || DEFAULT_TIMEOUT;
  }

  async request<T>(
    endpoint: string,
    options: FetchOptions = {}
  ): Promise<FetchResponse<T>> {
    const url = `${this.baseURL}${endpoint}`;
    const {
      method = 'GET',
      headers = {},
      body,
      params,
      timeout = this.timeout,
      signal,
    } = options;

    // Build query string
    let urlWithParams = url;
    if (params) {
      const searchParams = new URLSearchParams();
      Object.entries(params).forEach(([key, value]) => {
        if (value !== undefined && value !== null) {
          searchParams.append(key, String(value));
        }
      });
      const queryString = searchParams.toString();
      if (queryString) {
        urlWithParams = `${url}?${queryString}`;
      }
    }

    // AbortController for timeout
    const controller = new AbortController();
    const timeoutId = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), timeout);
    const finalSignal = signal ? this.combineSignals(signal, controller.signal) : controller.signal;

    try {
      const response = await fetch(urlWithParams, {
        method,
        headers: { ...this.defaultHeaders, ...headers },
        body: body ? JSON.stringify(body) : undefined,
        signal: finalSignal,
      });

      clearTimeout(timeoutId);

      if (!response.ok) {
        const errorData = await response.json().catch(() => ({}));
        throw new FetchError(
          response.status,
          response.statusText,
          errorData
        );
      }

      const data = await response.json();
      return { data, status: response.status };
    } catch (error) {
      clearTimeout(timeoutId);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  get<T>(
    endpoint: string,
    options?: Omit<FetchOptions, 'method' | 'body'>
  ): Promise<FetchResponse<T>> {
    return this.request<T>(endpoint, { ...options, method: 'GET' });
  }

  post<T>(
    endpoint: string,
    body: unknown,
    options?: Omit<FetchOptions, 'method' | 'body'>
  ): Promise<FetchResponse<T>> {
    return this.request<T>(endpoint, { ...options, method: 'POST', body });
  }

  put<T>(
    endpoint: string,
    body: unknown,
    options?: Omit<FetchOptions, 'method' | 'body'>
  ): Promise<FetchResponse<T>> {
    return this.request<T>(endpoint, { ...options, method: 'PUT', body });
  }

  delete<T>(
    endpoint: string,
    options?: Omit<FetchOptions, 'method' | 'body'>
  ): Promise<FetchResponse<T>> {
    return this.request<T>(endpoint, { ...options, method: 'DELETE' });
  }

  private combineSignals(...signals: AbortSignal[]): AbortSignal {
    const controller = new AbortController();
    const onAbort = () => controller.abort();
    for (const signal of signals) {
      if (signal.aborted) {
        onAbort();
        break;
      }
      signal.addEventListener('abort', onAbort, { once: true });
    }
    return controller.signal;
  }
}

export class FetchError extends Error {
  constructor(
    public status: number,
    public statusText: string,
    public data?: Record<string, unknown>
  ) {
    super(`Request failed with status ${status}: ${statusText}`);
    this.name = 'FetchError';
  }
}
```

```typescript
// shared/lib/fetch/types.ts
export interface FetchOptions {
  method?: 'GET' | 'POST' | 'PUT' | 'DELETE' | 'PATCH';
  headers?: Record<string, string>;
  body?: unknown;
  params?: Record<string, unknown>;
  timeout?: number;
  signal?: AbortSignal;
}

export interface FetchResponse<T> {
  data: T;
  status: number;
}
```

```typescript
// shared/lib/fetch/use-fetch.ts
import { FetchClient } from './fetch-client';
import type { FetchOptions, FetchResponse } from './types';

const client = new FetchClient(
  import.meta.env.VITE_API_BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:8000'
);

export function useFetch() {
  return {
    request: <T>(endpoint: string, options?: FetchOptions) =>
      client.request<T>(endpoint, options),
    get: <T>(endpoint: string, options?: Omit<FetchOptions, 'method' | 'body'>) =>
      client.get<T>(endpoint, options),
    post: <T>(endpoint: string, body: unknown, options?: Omit<FetchOptions, 'method' | 'body'>) =>
      client.post<T>(endpoint, body, options),
    put: <T>(endpoint: string, body: unknown, options?: Omit<FetchOptions, 'method' | 'body'>) =>
      client.put<T>(endpoint, body, options),
    delete: <T>(endpoint: string, options?: Omit<FetchOptions, 'method' | 'body'>) =>
      client.delete<T>(endpoint, options),
  };
}

export { client as fetchClient };
```

```typescript
// shared/api/uma/uma-api.ts
import { useFetch } from '../../lib/fetch';
import type {
  SelectRequest,
  SelectResponse,
  SQL2JSQLRequest,
  JSQL2SQLRequest,
  EntityListRequest,
  EntityListResponse,
  EntityDetailsRequest,
  EntityMetadata,
  ErrorResponse,
} from './types';

const { get, post } = useFetch();

export const umaApi = {
  /**
   * Execute JSQL query
   */
  async select(request: SelectRequest): Promise<SelectResponse> {
    const response = await post<SelectResponse>('/api/uma/select', request);
    return response.data;
  },

  /**
   * Convert SQL to JSQL
   */
  async sqlToJsql(request: SQL2JSQLRequest): Promise<Record<string, unknown>> {
    const response = await post<Record<string, unknown>>('/api/uma/transform/sql2jsql', request);
    return response.data;
  },

  /**
   * Convert JSQL to SQL
   */
  async jsqlToSql(request: JSQL2SQLRequest): Promise<{ sql: string }> {
    const response = await post<{ sql: string }>('/api/uma/transform/jsql2sql', request);
    return response.data;
  },

  /**
   * Get list of entities
   */
  async getEntityList(request?: EntityListRequest): Promise<EntityListResponse> {
    const response = await post<EntityListResponse>('/api/uma/meta/entity_list', request || {});
    return response.data;
  },

  /**
   * Get entity metadata
   */
  async getEntityDetails(request: EntityDetailsRequest): Promise<EntityMetadata> {
    const response = await post<EntityMetadata>('/api/uma/meta/entity_details', request);
    return response.data;
  },

  /**
   * Health check
   */
  async healthCheck(): Promise<{ status: string; service: string }> {
    const response = await get<{ status: string; service: string }>('/health');
    return response.data;
  },
};
```

```typescript
// features/sql-editor/ui/SqlEditor.vue
<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, onMounted, onUnmounted, watch } from 'vue';
import { EditorView, basicSetup } from 'codemirror';
import { sql, SQLDialect } from '@codemirror/lang-sql';
import { oneDark } from '@codemirror/theme-one-dark';
import { keymap } from '@codemirror/view';
import { defaultKeymap, indentWithTab } from '@codemirror/commands';

interface Props {
  modelValue: string;
  dialect?: 'postgresql' | 'mysql' | 'sqlite' | 'mssql' | 'generic';
  theme?: 'light' | 'dark';
  readonly?: boolean;
  placeholder?: string;
}

interface Emits {
  (e: 'update:modelValue', value: string): void;
  (e: 'execute'): void;
  (e: 'valid', isValid: boolean): void;
}

const props = withDefaults(defineProps<Props>(), {
  dialect: 'generic',
  theme: 'light',
  readonly: false,
  placeholder: 'Enter SQL query...',
});

const emit = defineEmits<Emits>();

const editorContainer = ref<HTMLElement>();
let editor: EditorView | null = null;

// Dialect mapping
const dialectMap: Record<string, SQLDialect> = {
  postgresql: PostgreSQL,
  mysql: MySQL,
  sqlite: SQLite,
  mssql: MSSQL,
  generic: StandardSQL,
};

onMounted(() => {
  if (!editorContainer.value) return;

  editor = new EditorView({
    doc: props.modelValue,
    extensions: [
      basicSetup,
      sql({ dialect: dialectMap[props.dialect] || StandardSQL }),
      props.theme === 'dark' ? oneDark : [],
      EditorView.lineWrapping,
      keymap.of([
        ...defaultKeymap,
        indentWithTab,
        { key: 'Ctrl-Enter', run: () => { emit('execute'); return true; } },
      ]),
      EditorView.editable.of(!props.readonly),
      EditorView.placeholder(props.placeholder),
      EditorView.updateListener.of((update) => {
        if (update.docChanged) {
          emit('update:modelValue', update.state.doc.toString());
          emit('valid', update.state.doc.toString().trim().length > 0);
        }
      }),
    ],
    parent: editorContainer.value,
  });
});

onUnmounted(() => {
  editor?.destroy();
});

watch(() => props.modelValue, (newValue) => {
  if (editor && newValue !== editor.state.doc.toString()) {
    editor.dispatch({
      changes: { from: 0, to: editor.state.doc.length, insert: newValue },
    });
  }
});

watch(() => props.dialect, (newDialect) => {
  if (editor) {
    // Reinitialize with new dialect
    // This is simplified; actual implementation may need more care
    const extensions = editor.state.facet(EditorView.editorAttributes);
    // Update dialect extension
  }
});

function focus() {
  editor?.focus();
}

function getValue() {
  return editor?.state.doc.toString() ?? '';
}

defineExpose({
  focus,
  getValue,
});
</script>

<template>
  <div ref="editorContainer" class="sql-editor"></div>
</template>

<style scoped>
.sql-editor {
  height: 100%;
  width: 100%;
  overflow: hidden;
}
</style>
```

```typescript
// features/jsql-editor/ui/JsqlEditor.vue
<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, onMounted, onUnmounted, watch } from 'vue';
import { EditorView, basicSetup } from 'codemirror';
import { javascript } from '@codemirror/lang-javascript';
import { oneDark } from '@codemirror/theme-one-dark';
import { keymap } from '@codemirror/view';
import { defaultKeymap, indentWithTab } from '@codemirror/commands';

interface Props {
  modelValue: Record<string, unknown> | null;
  theme?: 'light' | 'dark';
  readonly?: boolean;
  placeholder?: string;
}

interface Emits {
  (e: 'update:modelValue', value: Record<string, unknown> | null): void;
  (e: 'execute'): void;
  (e: 'valid', isValid: boolean): void;
  (e: 'error', error: string | null): void;
}

const props = withDefaults(defineProps<Props>(), {
  modelValue: null,
  theme: 'light',
  readonly: false,
  placeholder: 'Enter JSQL query as JSON...',
});

const emit = defineEmits<Emits>();

const editorContainer = ref<HTMLElement>();
let editor: EditorView | null = null;

onMounted(() => {
  if (!editorContainer.value) return;

  const initialValue = props.modelValue ? JSON.stringify(props.modelValue, null, 2) : '';

  editor = new EditorView({
    doc: initialValue,
    extensions: [
      basicSetup,
      javascript(),
      props.theme === 'dark' ? oneDark : [],
      EditorView.lineWrapping,
      keymap.of([
        ...defaultKeymap,
        indentWithTab,
        { key: 'Ctrl-Enter', run: () => { emit('execute'); return true; } },
      ]),
      EditorView.editable.of(!props.readonly),
      EditorView.placeholder(props.placeholder),
      EditorView.updateListener.of((update) => {
        if (update.docChanged) {
          const value = update.state.doc.toString();
          try {
            if (value.trim().length === 0) {
              emit('update:modelValue', null);
              emit('valid', false);
              emit('error', null);
            } else {
              const parsed = JSON.parse(value) as Record<string, unknown>;
              emit('update:modelValue', parsed);
              emit('valid', true);
              emit('error', null);
            }
          } catch (e) {
            emit('error', e instanceof Error ? e.message : 'Invalid JSON');
            emit('valid', false);
          }
        }
      }),
    ],
    parent: editorContainer.value,
  });
});

onUnmounted(() => {
  editor?.destroy();
});

watch(() => props.modelValue, (newValue) => {
  if (editor) {
    const jsonValue = newValue ? JSON.stringify(newValue, null, 2) : '';
    if (jsonValue !== editor.state.doc.toString()) {
      editor.dispatch({
        changes: { from: 0, to: editor.state.doc.length, insert: jsonValue },
      });
    }
  }
});

function format() {
  if (editor) {
    const current = editor.state.doc.toString();
    if (current.trim().length > 0) {
      try {
        const parsed = JSON.parse(current);
        const formatted = JSON.stringify(parsed, null, 2);
        editor.dispatch({
          changes: { from: 0, to: editor.state.doc.length, insert: formatted },
        });
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('Failed to format JSON:', e);
      }
    }
  }
}

function focus() {
  editor?.focus();
}

function getValue() {
  return editor?.state.doc.toString() ?? '';
}

defineExpose({
  focus,
  getValue,
  format,
});
</script>

<template>
  <div ref="editorContainer" class="jsql-editor"></div>
</template>

<style scoped>
.jsql-editor {
  height: 100%;
  width: 100%;
  overflow: hidden;
}
</style>
```

```typescript
// features/sql-editor/ui/EditorToolbar.vue
<script setup lang="ts">
import { Button } from '../../../shared/ui/button';
import { 
  Play, 
  Copy, 
  Trash2, 
  RotateCw, 
  ArrowRightLeft,
  FileCode,
  CheckCircle,
  XCircle
} from 'lucide-vue-next';

interface Props {
  type: 'sql' | 'jsql';
  canExecute?: boolean;
  isValid?: boolean;
  isExecuting?: boolean;
}

interface Emits {
  (e: 'execute'): void;
  (e: 'convert'): void;
  (e: 'format'): void;
  (e: 'clear'): void;
  (e: 'copy'): void;
}

defineProps<Props>();
const emit = defineEmits<Emits>();
</script>

<template>
  <div class="editor-toolbar flex items-center gap-2 p-2 border-b">
    <Button
      variant="default"
      size="sm"
      :disabled="!canExecute || isExecuting"
      @click="emit('execute')"
    >
      <Play v-if="!isExecuting" class="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
      <RotateCw v-else class="w-4 h-4 mr-2 animate-spin" />
      {{ type === 'sql' ? 'Run SQL' : 'Run JSQL' }}
    </Button>

    <Button
      v-if="type === 'sql'"
      variant="outline"
      size="sm"
      :disabled="!canExecute"
      @click="emit('convert')"
    >
      <ArrowRightLeft class="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
      Convert to JSQL
    </Button>

    <Button
      v-if="type === 'jsql'"
      variant="outline"
      size="sm"
      :disabled="!canExecute"
      @click="emit('format')"
    >
      <FileCode class="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
      Format JSON
    </Button>

    <div class="flex-1"></div>

    <CheckCircle 
      v-if="isValid !== undefined && isValid" 
      class="w-5 h-5 text-green-500" 
    />
    <XCircle 
      v-else-if="isValid !== undefined && !isValid" 
      class="w-5 h-5 text-red-500" 
    />

    <Button
      variant="ghost"
      size="sm"
      @click="emit('copy')"
    >
      <Copy class="w-4 h-4" />
    </Button>

    <Button
      variant="ghost"
      size="sm"
      @click="emit('clear')"
    >
      <Trash2 class="w-4 h-4" />
    </Button>
  </div>
</template>
```

```typescript
// features/query-execution/lib/use-query-executor.ts
import { ref, computed } from 'vue';
import { useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/vue-query';
import { umaApi } from '../../../../shared/api/uma';
import type { SelectRequest, SelectResponse } from '../../../../shared/api/uma/types';

interface UseQueryExecutorOptions {
  onSuccess?: (result: SelectResponse) => void;
  onError?: (error: Error) => void;
}

export function useQueryExecutor(options?: UseQueryExecutorOptions) {
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();

  const mutation = useMutation({
    mutationKey: ['uma', 'select'],
    mutationFn: async (request: SelectRequest) => {
      return await umaApi.select(request);
    },
    onSuccess: (result) => {
      options?.onSuccess?.(result);
    },
    onError: (error) => {
      options?.onError?.(error instanceof Error ? error : new Error(String(error)));
    },
  });

  const executeJsql = async (
    jsql: Record<string, unknown>,
    params?: Record<string, unknown> | null
  ): Promise<SelectResponse> => {
    const request: SelectRequest = {
      jsql,
      params: params || undefined,
    };
    return await mutation.mutateAsync(request);
  };

  const executeSql = async (
    sql: string,
    dialect: string = 'generic'
  ): Promise<SelectResponse> => {
    // First convert SQL to JSQL
    const jsql = await umaApi.sqlToJsql({
      data: sql,
      dialect,
    });

    // Then execute the JSQL
    return await executeJsql(jsql);
  };

  return {
    executeJsql,
    executeSql,
    isExecuting: computed(() => mutation.isPending.value),
    error: computed(() => mutation.error),
  };
}
```

```typescript
// features/query-converter/lib/use-query-converter.ts
import { ref, computed } from 'vue';
import { useMutation } from '@tanstack/vue-query';
import { umaApi } from '../../../../shared/api/uma';
import type { SQL2JSQLRequest, JSQL2SQLRequest } from '../../../../shared/api/uma/types';

interface UseQueryConverterOptions {
  onSuccess?: () => void;
  onError?: (error: Error) => void;
}

export function useQueryConverter(options?: UseQueryConverterOptions) {
  const sqlToJsqlMutation = useMutation({
    mutationKey: ['uma', 'sql-to-jsql'],
    mutationFn: async (request: SQL2JSQLRequest) => {
      return await umaApi.sqlToJsql(request);
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      options?.onSuccess?.();
    },
    onError: (error) => {
      options?.onError?.(error instanceof Error ? error : new Error(String(error)));
    },
  });

  const jsqlToSqlMutation = useMutation({
    mutationKey: ['uma', 'jsql-to-sql'],
    mutationFn: async (request: JSQL2SQLRequest) => {
      return await umaApi.jsqlToSql(request);
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      options?.onSuccess?.();
    },
    onError: (error) => {
      options?.onError?.(error instanceof Error ? error : new Error(String(error)));
    },
  });

  const sqlToJsql = async (
    sql: string,
    dialect: string = 'generic'
  ): Promise<Record<string, unknown>> => {
    return await sqlToJsqlMutation.mutateAsync({
      data: sql,
      dialect,
    });
  };

  const jsqlToSql = async (
    jsql: Record<string, unknown>,
    dialect: string = 'generic'
  ): Promise<string> => {
    const result = await jsqlToSqlMutation.mutateAsync({
      data: jsql,
      dialect,
    });
    return result.sql;
  };

  return {
    sqlToJsql,
    jsqlToSql,
    isConverting: computed(() => 
      sqlToJsqlMutation.isPending.value || jsqlToSqlMutation.isPending.value
    ),
    error: computed(() => 
      sqlToJsqlMutation.error || jsqlToSqlMutation.error
    ),
  };
}
```

```typescript
// –í MainPage.vue
const handleRunSql = async () => {
  try {
    // 1. Convert SQL to JSQL
    const jsql = await converter.sqlToJsql(sqlQuery.value, dialect.value);
    
    // 2. Update JSQL editor
    jsqlQuery.value = jsql;
    
    // 3. Execute JSQL
    const result = await executor.executeJsql(jsql);
    
    // 4. Update results
    queryResults.value = result;
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to execute SQL:', error);
  }
};
```

```typescript
const handleRunJsql = async () => {
  try {
    // 1. Optionally get SQL for debug
    const sqlResult = await converter.jsqlToSql(jsqlQuery.value!, dialect.value);
    generatedSql.value = sqlResult;
    
    // 2. Execute JSQL
    const result = await executor.executeJsql(jsqlQuery.value!);
    
    // 3. Update results
    queryResults.value = result;
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to execute JSQL:', error);
  }
};

  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to convert SQL to JSQL:', error);

};

  try {
    const sql = await converter.jsqlToSql(jsqlQuery.value!, dialect.value);
    generatedSql.value = sql; // Show in debug panel
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to convert JSQL to SQL:', error);

```typescript
// features/query-results/ui/QueryResultsTable.vue
<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, computed, watch, onMounted, onUnmounted } from 'vue';
import { AgGridVue } from 'ag-grid-vue3';
import { 
  type ColDef, 
  type GridOptions, 
  type GetRowsParams, 
  GridApi,
  ModuleRegistry,
  ClientSideRowModelModule,
  InfiniteRowModelModule,
} from 'ag-grid-community';
import type { SelectResponse } from '../../../../shared/api/uma/types';

// Import AG Grid styles
import 'ag-grid-community/styles/ag-grid.css';
import 'ag-grid-community/styles/ag-theme-quartz.css';

// Register modules
ModuleRegistry.registerModules([ClientSideRowModelModule, InfiniteRowModelModule]);

interface Props {
  results: SelectResponse | null;
  loading?: boolean;
  infinite?: boolean; // Enable infinite scroll
  pageSize?: number;
}

const props = withDefaults(defineProps<Props>(), {
  loading: false,
  infinite: false,
  pageSize: 100,
});

const gridApi = ref<GridApi>();
const columnDefs = ref<ColDef[]>([]);
const rowData = ref<Record<string, unknown>[]>([]);
const loading = ref(false);

// Determine column types based on metadata
const getColDef = (meta: { type: string; name: string }): ColDef => {
  const type = meta.type.toLowerCase();
  
  // Map SQL types to AG Grid cell types
  if (type.includes('int') || type.includes('numeric') || type.includes('decimal')) {
    return {
      headerName: meta.name,
      field: meta.name,
      type: 'numericColumn',
      filter: 'agNumberColumnFilter',
    };
  }
  
  if (type.includes('bool')) {
    return {
      headerName: meta.name,
      field: meta.name,
      type: 'booleanColumn',
      filter: 'agSetColumnFilter',
      cellRenderer: (params: { value: unknown }) => {
        if (params.value === null || params.value === undefined) return '';
        return params.value ? '‚úì' : '‚úó';
      },
    };
  }
  
  if (type.includes('date') || type.includes('time') || type.includes('timestamp')) {
    return {
      headerName: meta.name,
      field: meta.name,
      type: 'dateColumn',
      filter: 'agDateColumnFilter',
      valueFormatter: (params: { value: unknown }) => {
        if (!params.value) return '';
        return new Date(String(params.value)).toLocaleString();
      },
    };
  }
  
  // Default: text column
  return {
    headerName: meta.name,
    field: meta.name,
    type: 'textColumn',
    filter: 'agTextColumnFilter',
    resizable: true,
    sortable: true,
  };
};

// Update column definitions when results change
watch(() => props.results, (newResults) => {
  if (newResults?.meta) {
    columnDefs.value = newResults.meta.map(getColDef);
    rowData.value = newResults.data;
  } else {
    columnDefs.value = [];
    rowData.value = [];
  }
});

// Grid options
const gridOptions = computed<GridOptions>(() => ({
  columnDefs: columnDefs.value,
  rowData: rowData.value,
  rowModelType: props.infinite ? 'infinite' : 'clientSide',
  cacheBlockSize: props.pageSize,
  maxBlocksInCache: 10,
  maxConcurrentDatasourceRequests: 1,
  infiniteInitialRowCount: props.infinite ? props.pageSize : undefined,
  animateRows: true,
  enableCellTextSelection: true,
  defaultColDef: {
    resizable: true,
    sortable: true,
    filter: true,
    flex: 1,
    minWidth: 100,
  },
  theme: 'quartz',
  // Custom theme variables for Tailwind integration
  getRowStyle: () => ({
    backgroundColor: 'var(--ag-row-background-color)',
    fontFamily: 'var(--ag-font-family)',
  }),
}));

// Infinite datasource (if enabled)
const datasource = {
  async getRows(params: GetRowsParams) {
    try {
      loading.value = true;
      
      const { startRow, endRow } = params;
      const offset = startRow;
      const limit = endRow - startRow;
      
      // TODO: Implement actual pagination logic here
      // const result = await umaApi.select({ jsql: ..., params: { offset, limit } });
      
      // For now, use existing data
      const rows = rowData.value.slice(startRow, endRow);
      const lastRow = rowData.value.length;
      
      loading.value = false;
      params.successCallback(rows, lastRow);
    } catch (error) {
      loading.value = false;
      params.failCallback();
    }
  },
};

watch(() => props.infinite, (infinite) => {
  if (infinite && gridApi.value) {
    gridApi.value.setGridOption('datasource', datasource);
  }
});

function onGridReady(params: { api: GridApi }) {
  gridApi.value = params.api;
  
  if (props.infinite) {
    gridApi.value.setGridOption('datasource', datasource);
  }
}

function exportToCsv() {
  gridApi.value?.exportDataAsCsv();
}

function clearSelection() {
  gridApi.value?.deselectAll();
}

function sizeColumnsToFit() {
  gridApi.value?.sizeColumnsToFit();
}

defineExpose({
  exportToCsv,
  clearSelection,
  sizeColumnsToFit,
});
</script>

<template>
  <div class="query-results-table h-full w-full">
    <AgGridVue
      v-if="results"
      :grid-options="gridOptions"
      :class="['ag-theme-quartz', 'h-full', 'w-full']"
      style="--ag-header-height: 40px; --ag-row-height: 40px;"
      @grid-ready="onGridReady"
    />
    <div
      v-else-if="loading"
      class="flex items-center justify-center h-full text-gray-500"
    >
      <div class="animate-spin rounded-full h-12 w-12 border-b-2 border-gray-900"></div>
    </div>
    <div
      v-else
      class="flex items-center justify-center h-full text-gray-500"
    >
      <p>No results to display</p>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<style scoped>
/* Custom AG Grid theme variables for Tailwind integration */
:deep(.ag-theme-quartz) {
  --ag-foreground-color: rgb(23, 23, 23);
  --ag-background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);
  --ag-header-background-color: rgb(243, 244, 246);
  --ag-odd-row-background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);
  --ag-row-hover-color: rgb(243, 244, 246);
  --ag-border-color: rgb(229, 231, 235);
  --ag-header-foreground-color: rgb(17, 24, 39);
  --ag-cell-horizontal-border: rgb(229, 231, 235);
  --ag-font-family: ui-sans-serif, system-ui, -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, 'Helvetica Neue', Arial;
  --ag-font-size: 14px;
  --ag-row-height: 40px;
  --ag-header-height: 40px;
}

/* Dark theme support */
@media (prefers-color-scheme: dark) {
  :deep(.ag-theme-quartz) {
    --ag-foreground-color: rgb(243, 244, 246);
    --ag-background-color: rgb(17, 24, 39);
    --ag-header-background-color: rgb(31, 41, 55);
    --ag-odd-row-background-color: rgb(17, 24, 39);
    --ag-row-hover-color: rgb(31, 41, 55);
    --ag-border-color: rgb(55, 65, 81);
    --ag-header-foreground-color: rgb(243, 244, 246);
    --ag-cell-horizontal-border: rgb(55, 65, 81);
  }
}
</style>

```typescript
// features/schema-explorer/ui/SchemaExplorer.vue
<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, onMounted } from 'vue';
import { useQuery } from '@tanstack/vue-query';
import { umaApi } from '../../../../shared/api/uma';
import type { EntityListResponse, EntityMetadata } from '../../../../shared/api/uma/types';
import { Button } from '../../../shared/ui/button';
import { ChevronRight, ChevronDown, Database, Table, Key } from 'lucide-vue-next';

interface Props {
  onInsertColumn?: (table: string, column: string) => void;
  namespace?: string;
}

const props = defineProps<Props>();

const expandedNodes = ref<Set<string>>(new Set());
const selectedEntity = ref<string | null>(null);

// Fetch entities list
const { data: entities, isLoading: loadingEntities } = useQuery({
  queryKey: ['uma', 'entities', props.namespace],
  queryFn: async () => {
    return await umaApi.getEntityList({ namespace: props.namespace });
  },
});

// Fetch selected entity details
const { data: entityMetadata, isLoading: loadingMetadata } = useQuery({
  queryKey: ['uma', 'entity', selectedEntity.value],
  queryFn: async () => {
    if (!selectedEntity.value) return null;
    return await umaApi.getEntityDetails({ entity_name: selectedEntity.value });
  },
  enabled: !!selectedEntity.value,
});

function toggleNode(node: string) {
  if (expandedNodes.value.has(node)) {
    expandedNodes.value.delete(node);
  } else {
    expandedNodes.value.add(node);
  }
}

function selectEntity(entity: string) {
  selectedEntity.value = entity;
  expandedNodes.value.add(entity);
}

function insertColumn(column: string) {
  if (selectedEntity.value && props.onInsertColumn) {
    props.onInsertColumn(selectedEntity.value, column);
  }
}

function insertEntity(entity: string) {
  if (props.onInsertColumn) {
    props.onInsertColumn(entity, '');
  }
}
</script>

<template>
  <div class="schema-explorer h-full flex flex-col bg-white dark:bg-gray-900 border-r">
    <div class="p-3 border-b">
      <h2 class="font-semibold text-sm">Schema Explorer</h2>
    </div>

    <div v-if="loadingEntities" class="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center">
      <div class="animate-spin rounded-full h-8 w-8 border-b-2 border-gray-900"></div>
    </div>

    <div v-else class="flex-1 overflow-auto p-2">
      <div v-if="entities?.entities.length === 0" class="text-sm text-gray-500 text-center py-4">
        No entities found
      </div>

      <div v-else class="space-y-1">
        <div 
          v-for="entity in entities?.entities" 
          :key="entity"
          class="entity-node"
        >
          <div
            class="flex items-center gap-2 px-2 py-1 rounded hover:bg-gray-100 dark:hover:bg-gray-800 cursor-pointer"
            @click="selectEntity(entity)"
          >
            <ChevronRight
              v-if="!expandedNodes.has(entity)"
              class="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400"
            />
            <ChevronDown
              v-else
              class="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400"
            />
            <Database class="w-4 h-4 text-blue-500" />
            <span class="text-sm">{{ entity }}</span>
          </div>

          <div v-if="expandedNodes.has(entity)" class="ml-6 space-y-1">
            <div v-if="loadingMetadata" class="px-2 py-1 text-sm text-gray-500">
              Loading...
            </div>

            <div v-else-if="entityMetadata?.name === entity">
              <div
                v-for="column in entityMetadata.columns"
                :key="column.name"
                class="flex items-center gap-2 px-2 py-1 rounded hover:bg-gray-100 dark:hover:bg-gray-800 cursor-pointer group"
                @click="insertColumn(column.name)"
              >
                <Table class="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400" />
                <Key 
                  v-if="column.primary_key"
                  class="w-3 h-3 text-yellow-500"
                />
                <span class="text-sm">{{ column.name }}</span>
                <span class="text-xs text-gray-500">{{ column.type }}</span>
                <span class="ml-auto opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 text-xs text-blue-500">
                  Insert
                </span>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<style scoped>
.entity-node {
  user-select: none;
}
</style>
```

```typescript
// pages/main/ui/MainPage.vue
<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, computed } from 'vue';
import { ResizablePanel, ResizableHandle } from '../../shared/ui/resizable';
import { Tabs, TabsList, TabsTrigger, TabsContent } from '../../shared/ui/tabs';
import SqlEditor from '../../features/sql-editor/ui/SqlEditor.vue';
import JsqlEditor from '../../features/jsql-editor/ui/JsqlEditor.vue';
import EditorToolbar from '../../features/sql-editor/ui/EditorToolbar.vue';
import QueryResultsTable from '../../features/query-results/ui/QueryResultsTable.vue';
import ResultsHeader from '../../features/query-results/ui/ResultsHeader.vue';
import ResultsToolbar from '../../features/query-results/ui/ResultsToolbar.vue';
import SchemaExplorer from '../../features/schema-explorer/ui/SchemaExplorer.vue';
import { useQueryExecutor } from '../../features/query-execution/lib/use-query-executor';
import { useQueryConverter } from '../../features/query-converter/lib/use-query-converter';
import { useLocalStorage } from '../../shared/lib/local-storage/use-local-storage';

// State
const sqlQuery = useLocalStorage('uma-sql-query', '');
const jsqlQuery = useLocalStorage('uma-jsql-query', null as Record<string, unknown> | null);
const dialect = useLocalStorage('uma-dialect', 'generic');
const generatedSql = ref<string | null>(null);
const queryResults = ref<ReturnType<typeof import('../../shared/api/uma/types').SelectResponse> | null>(null);
const executionTime = ref<number>(0);
const activeTab = ref('sql');
const showSchemaExplorer = useLocalStorage('uma-show-schema-explorer', true);

// Query executor and converter
const executor = useQueryExecutor({
  onSuccess: (result) => {
    queryResults.value = result;
  },
});

const converter = useQueryConverter();

// Event handlers
const handleRunSql = async () => {
  const startTime = performance.now();
  try {
    // Convert SQL to JSQL
    const jsql = await converter.sqlToJsql(sqlQuery.value, dialect.value);
    jsqlQuery.value = jsql;
    
    // Execute JSQL
    const result = await executor.executeJsql(jsql);
    
    executionTime.value = Math.round(performance.now() - startTime);
    activeTab.value = 'jsql';
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to execute SQL:', error);
  }
};

const handleRunJsql = async () => {
  const startTime = performance.now();
  try {
    // Optionally get SQL for debug
    const sql = await converter.jsqlToSql(jsqlQuery.value!, dialect.value);
    generatedSql.value = sql;
    
    // Execute JSQL
    const result = await executor.executeJsql(jsqlQuery.value!);
    
    executionTime.value = Math.round(performance.now() - startTime);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to execute JSQL:', error);
  }
};

const handleConvertSqlToJsql = async () => {
  try {
    const jsql = await converter.sqlToJsql(sqlQuery.value, dialect.value);
    jsqlQuery.value = jsql;
    activeTab.value = 'jsql';
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to convert SQL to JSQL:', error);
  }
};

const handleConvertJsqlToSql = async () => {
  try {
    const sql = await converter.jsqlToSql(jsqlQuery.value!, dialect.value);
    generatedSql.value = sql;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to convert JSQL to SQL:', error);
  }
};

const handleClearSql = () => {
  sqlQuery.value = '';
};

const handleClearJsql = () => {
  jsqlQuery.value = null;
};

const handleCopySql = () => {
  navigator.clipboard.writeText(sqlQuery.value);
};

const handleCopyJsql = () => {
  navigator.clipboard.writeText(JSON.stringify(jsqlQuery.value, null, 2));
};

const handleExportResults = () => {
  // TODO: Implement export
};

const handleClearResults = () => {
  queryResults.value = null;
  generatedSql.value = null;
  executionTime.value = 0;
};

const handleShowSql = () => {
  // Show SQL in dialog
};

const handleInsertColumn = (table: string, column: string) => {
  const text = column ? `${table}.${column}` : table;
  if (activeTab.value === 'sql') {
    sqlQuery.value += ` ${text}`;
  } else {
    // Insert into JSQL (more complex)
  }
};

// Computed
const sqlEditorValid = computed(() => sqlQuery.value.trim().length > 0);
const jsqlEditorValid = computed(() => jsqlQuery.value !== null);
</script>

<template>
  <div class="main-page h-screen flex">
    <!-- Schema Explorer Sidebar -->
    <SchemaExplorer
      v-if="showSchemaExplorer"
      :namespace="null"
      :on-insert-column="handleInsertColumn"
      class="w-64 flex-shrink-0"
    />

    <!-- Main Content -->
    <div class="flex-1 flex flex-col overflow-hidden">
      <!-- Editors Section (40% height) -->
      <ResizablePanel class="h-2/5 border-b">
        <Tabs v-model="activeTab" class="h-full flex flex-col">
          <div class="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 border-b bg-gray-50 dark:bg-gray-800">
            <TabsList>
              <TabsTrigger value="sql">SQL</TabsTrigger>
              <TabsTrigger value="jsql">JSQL</TabsTrigger>
            </TabsList>

            <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
              <label class="text-sm text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-400">Dialect:</label>
              <select
                v-model="dialect"
                class="text-sm rounded border px-2 py-1 bg-white dark:bg-gray-900"
              >
                <option value="generic">Generic</option>
                <option value="postgresql">PostgreSQL</option>
                <option value="mysql">MySQL</option>
                <option value="sqlite">SQLite</option>
                <option value="mssql">SQL Server</option>
              </select>
            </div>
          </div>

          <TabsContent value="sql" class="flex-1 flex flex-col m-0">
            <EditorToolbar
              type="sql"
              :can-execute="sqlEditorValid"
              :is-executing="executor.isExecuting.value"
              @execute="handleRunSql"
              @convert="handleConvertSqlToJsql"
              @clear="handleClearSql"
              @copy="handleCopySql"
            />
            <SqlEditor
              v-model="sqlQuery"
              :dialect="dialect"
              @execute="handleRunSql"
            />
          </TabsContent>

          <TabsContent value="jsql" class="flex-1 flex flex-col m-0">
            <EditorToolbar
              type="jsql"
              :can-execute="jsqlEditorValid"
              :is-executing="executor.isExecuting.value"
              @execute="handleRunJsql"
              @format="() => {}"
              @clear="handleClearJsql"
              @copy="handleCopyJsql"
            />
            <JsqlEditor
              v-model="jsqlQuery"
              @execute="handleRunJsql"
            />
          </TabsContent>
        </Tabs>
      </ResizablePanel>

      <ResizableHandle />

      <!-- Results Section (60% height) -->
      <ResizablePanel class="h-3/5 flex flex-col">
        <ResultsHeader
          :results="queryResults"
          :execution-time="executionTime"
          :query-type="activeTab as 'sql' | 'jsql'"
        >
          <ResultsToolbar
            :has-results="!!queryResults"
            @export="handleExportResults"
            @clear="handleClearResults"
            @show-sql="handleShowSql"
          />
        </ResultsHeader>

        <QueryResultsTable
          :results="queryResults"
          :loading="executor.isExecuting.value"
          :infinite="false"
        />
      </ResizablePanel>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<style scoped>
.main-page {
  background: white;
  color: rgb(23, 23, 23);
}

@media (prefers-color-scheme: dark) {
  .main-page {
    background: rgb(17, 24, 39);
    color: rgb(243, 244, 246);
  }
}
</style>
```

```json
{
  "name": "uma-frontend-demo",
